matplotlib demo

Hello, this page will showcase the dashboard for issues

Hello, this page will showcase the main dashboard!

#Initializing Workspace
import requests
import datetime
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

#API Function
def fetch_api(endpoint):
 url = f"https://api.github.com/repos/jspsych/jsPsych/{endpoint}"
 final_data=[]
 while url:
  response = requests.get(url)
  data = response.json()
  for item in data:
    final_data.append(item)
  if 'next' in response.links:
    url = response.links['next']['url']
  else:
    break

  return final_data
ret_data = fetch_api(f"issues?false&state=all&per_page=100")
ret_data

  'body': "this PR clears the dom after every individual test. the expected pattern of using `startTimeline` in the `test-utils` package is to deconstruct the tuple given and take out `displayElement` in order to directly query the experiment's display element. however, some plugins still query `document` directly, which isn't optimal as the dom is not cleared, meaning there are multiple jsPsych display elements on the dom at a given time. this results in some interesting edge cases where the wrong button is queried, or one test failing means every next test that interacts with the `document` fails.\r\n\r\nthis is a small, simple update in order to allow tests to both query `document` and `displayElement` without having to deal with this behavior by making sure the DOM is wiped before each individual test.",

  'body': 'The documentation on [timelines](https://www.jspsych.org/v7/overview/timeline/) provides an example section on dynamic parameters with anonymous functions, which allows the user to access potentially multiple timeline variables and combine them into one parameter for a plugin. \r\n\r\nHowever I can\'t get the example code provided in the documentation to work: Even wrapped in an anonymous function, the `jsPsych.timelineVariable(\'myVariable\')` still just returns the object, so instead of displaying e.g. a string (as in the example below) it displays [object Object]. \r\n\r\nThe minimum example here is just copied from the docs. When I paste it into a fresh timeline the third plugin in the procedure results in a trial that just says [object Object] for the `name` part. The `img src =` part also does not work: from the \'file not found\' error in the console I can see that it\'s trying to load an image called `.../[object%20Object]`. \r\n\r\n\r\n```\r\nvar face_name_procedure = {\r\n    timeline: [\r\n        {\r\n            type: jsPsychHtmlKeyboardResponse,\r\n            stimulus: \'+\',\r\n            choices: "NO_KEYS",\r\n            trial_duration: 500\r\n        },\r\n        {\r\n            type: jsPsychHtmlKeyboardResponse,\r\n            stimulus: jsPsych.timelineVariable(\'name\'),\r\n            trial_duration: 1000,\r\n            choices: "NO_KEYS"\r\n        },\r\n        {\r\n            type: jsPsychHtmlKeyboardResponse,\r\n            stimulus: function(){\r\n                var html = `\r\n\t\t<img src="${jsPsych.timelineVariable(\'face\')}">\r\n\t\t<p>${jsPsych.timelineVariable(\'name\', true)}</p>`;\r\n                return html;\r\n            },          \r\n            choices: "NO_KEYS",\r\n            trial_duration: 2500\r\n        }\r\n    ],\r\n    timeline_variables: [\r\n        { face: \'person-1.jpg\', name: \'Alex\' },\r\n        { face: \'person-2.jpg\', name: \'Beth\' },\r\n        { face: \'person-3.jpg\', name: \'Chad\' },\r\n        { face: \'person-4.jpg\', name: \'Dave\' }\r\n    ]\r\n}\r\n```\r\n\r\nThis is related to [this thread] (https://github.com/jspsych/jsPsych/discussions/2619), and I did try that solution as well, but it gave the same results  (replacing the stimulus with `stimulus : () => { return "Test name: " + jsPsych.timelineVariable("name") + "?"; },` \r\n\r\n\r\nThe work-around I\'ve been doing is to write independent functions which first iterate over the timeline_variables array, building the parameters that need to involve multiple variables, and then passing the final product as a timeline_variable. This way, no parameters are created dynamically in the actual plugin part: each parameter can be accessed with `jsPsych.timelineVariable()`. An example is below; however, it will not work for users who want to do truly dynamic parameters (e.g. make them dependent upon a participants\' previous response).\r\n\r\nI also would just like to understand what I\'m doing wrong when implementing the solution from the docs: Is there maybe some magic to how JsPsych should be initiated, to let jsPsych know that it should delay evaluating the variables until runtime? \r\n\r\nThank you for your help! \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nHacky work-around e.g. if you need to create a stimulus from multiple trial parameters: \r\n```\r\nconst jsPsych = initJsPsych();\r\n\r\n\r\nlet timeline = [];\r\n\r\n\r\ntimeline_building_blocks = [\r\n\t{ face: \'person-1.jpg\', name: \'Alex\' },\r\n\t{ face: \'person-2.jpg\', name: \'Beth\' },\r\n\t{ face: \'person-3.jpg\', name: \'Chad\' },\r\n\t{ face: \'person-4.jpg\', name: \'Dave\' }\r\n]\r\n// Loop over the list of timelinevariables, and build the stimulus, other parameters you want: \r\nmy_timeline_variables = []\r\ntimeline_building_blocks.forEach(trial => {\r\n\tvar stimulus = `Here is a name: ${trial.name} and an image: <img src="${trial.face}">`;\r\n\tmy_timeline_variables.push({\r\n\t\tstimulus: stimulus,\r\n\t})\r\n});\r\n\r\n// Then push my_timeline_variables to the timeline as normal, can be accessed with jsPsych.timelineVariable()\r\n// Since the dynamic part is over:\r\nvar face_name_procedure = {\r\n\ttimeline : [\r\n\t\t{\r\n\t\t\ttype: jsPsychHtmlKeyboardResponse, \r\n\t\t\tstimulus: jsPsych.timelineVariable(\'stimulus\'),\r\n\t\t\tchoices: "NO_KEYS",\r\n\t\t}],\r\n\t\ttimeline_variables : my_timeline_variables,\r\n}\r\n\r\n\r\ntimeline.push(face_name_procedure)\r\njsPsych.run(timeline);\r\n\r\n```\r\n\r\n',

  'body': "Qualtrics have overwritten/incorrectly polyfilled `Array.from()` such that it doesn't work, and so neither does jsPsych when run directly in Qualtrics. This PR then replaces uses of `Array.from()` in jsPsych with equivalent functions. So far, a wrapped spread operator `[...array]` is used in the KeyboardResponseAPI, and `Array.prototype.slice.call()` in the `maxdiff` and `free-sort` plugins. \r\n\r\nThere's also a single `Array.from()` call in `packages/plugin-sketchpad/src/index.ts`, although I can't get this to run on my own fork even in the original version outside of Qualtrics. It also features heavily in the webgazer examples and demos.\r\n\r\nProbably worth considering this doesn't do much for any extension, anything in contrib, or Survey-js etc, so Qualtrics compatibility isn't guaranteed, but atleast the core library can be used without dealing with an extra hosting site.\r\n\r\nFollows from https://github.com/jspsych/jsPsych/discussions/3347.",
